**NOTE**

- Teste ANCOVA para determinar se houve diferenças significativas no
  Teste de Vocabulario (medido usando pre- e pos-testes).
- ANCOVA test to determine whether there were significant differences in
  Vocabulary Test (measured using pre- and post-tests).

| score.vocab.pos |  38 | 0.5181143 | 0.3337478 | NO       | 0.9677383 | Shapiro-Wilk | 0.3345270 | ns       | YES       |
| score.vocab.pos |  47 | 0.4810028 | 0.6739412 | YES      | 0.9643070 | Shapiro-Wilk | 0.1592871 | ns       | YES       |
| score.vocab.pos |  47 | 0.5376331 | 0.6699308 | NO       | 0.9676559 | Shapiro-Wilk | 0.2153349 | ns       | YES       |
